</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC448" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="448" style="position:relative">  Each time you convey a covered work, the recipient automatically</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC449" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="449" style="position:relative">receives a license from the original licensors, to run, modify and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC450" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="450" style="position:relative">propagate that work, subject to this License.  You are not responsible</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC451" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="451" style="position:relative">for enforcing compliance by third parties with this License.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC452" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="452" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC453" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="453" style="position:relative">  An &quot;entity transaction&quot; is a transaction transferring control of an</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC454" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="454" style="position:relative">organization, or substantially all assets of one, or subdividing an</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC455" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="455" style="position:relative">organization, or merging organizations.  If propagation of a covered</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC456" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="456" style="position:relative">work results from an entity transaction, each party to that</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC457" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="457" style="position:relative">transaction who receives a copy of the work also receives whatever</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC458" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="458" style="position:relative">licenses to the work the party&#039;s predecessor in interest had or could</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC459" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="459" style="position:relative">give under the previous paragraph, plus a right to possession of the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC460" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="460" style="position:relative">Corresponding Source of the work from the predecessor in interest, if</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC461" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="461" style="position:relative">the predecessor has it or can get it with reasonable efforts.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC462" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="462" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC463" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="463" style="position:relative">  You may not impose any further restrictions on the exercise of the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC464" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="464" style="position:relative">rights granted or affirmed under this License.  For example, you may</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC465" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="465" style="position:relative">not impose a license fee, royalty, or other charge for exercise of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC466" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="466" style="position:relative">rights granted under this License, and you may not initiate litigation</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC467" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="467" style="position:relative">(including a cross-claim or counterclaim in a lawsuit) alleging that</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC468" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="468" style="position:relative">any patent claim is infringed by making, using, selling, offering for</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC469" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="469" style="position:relative">sale, or importing the Program or any portion of it.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC470" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="470" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC471" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="471" style="position:relative">  11. Patents.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC472" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="472" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC473" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="473" style="position:relative">  A &quot;contributor&quot; is a copyright holder who authorizes use under this</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC474" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="474" style="position:relative">License of the Program or a work on which the Program is based.  The</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC475" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="475" style="position:relative">work thus licensed is called the contributor&#039;s &quot;contributor version&quot;.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC476" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="476" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC477" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="477" style="position:relative">  A contributor&#039;s &quot;essential patent claims&quot; are all patent claims</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC478" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="478" style="position:relative">owned or controlled by the contributor, whether already acquired or</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC479" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="479" style="position:relative">hereafter acquired, that would be infringed by some manner, permitted</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC480" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="480" style="position:relative">by this License, of making, using, or selling its contributor version,</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC481" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="481" style="position:relative">but do not include claims that would be infringed only as a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC482" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="482" style="position:relative">consequence of further modification of the contributor version.  For</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC483" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="483" style="position:relative">purposes of this definition, &quot;control&quot; includes the right to grant</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC484" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="484" style="position:relative">patent sublicenses in a manner consistent with the requirements of</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC485" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="485" style="position:relative">this License.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC486" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="486" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC487" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="487" style="position:relative">  Each contributor grants you a non-exclusive, worldwide, royalty-free</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC488" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="488" style="position:relative">patent license under the contributor&#039;s essential patent claims, to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC489" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="489" style="position:relative">make, use, sell, offer for sale, import and otherwise run, modify and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC490" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="490" style="position:relative">propagate the contents of its contributor version.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC491" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="491" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC492" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="492" style="position:relative">  In the following three paragraphs, a &quot;patent license&quot; is any express</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC493" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="493" style="position:relative">agreement or commitment, however denominated, not to enforce a patent</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC494" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="494" style="position:relative">(such as an express permission to practice a patent or covenant not to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC495" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="495" style="position:relative">sue for patent infringement).  To &quot;grant&quot; such a patent license to a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC496" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="496" style="position:relative">party means to make such an agreement or commitment not to enforce a</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC497" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="497" style="position:relative">patent against the party.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC498" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="498" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC499" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="499" to extend the patent</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC507" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" </div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC521" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="521" style="position:relative">  A patent license is &quot;discriminatory&quot; if it does not include within</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC522" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="522" style="position:relative">the scope of its coverage, prohibits the exercise of, or is</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC523" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="523" style="position:relative">conditioned on the non-exercise of one or more of the rights that are</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC524" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="524" style="position:relative">specifically granted under this License.
